et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then they are pushed against each other in order to extract the tooth, and the knuckles are used for support on both sides, as is the form:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if a part of it remains, then anoint some of his fingers with oil, and push them into that part, and pull on the other part.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if nothing remains, then place this knuckle or a higher one in position, and do this until it comes out completely.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement,	And if one hand comes before the other, and it cannot be returned due to the tightness,
si covient que tu envoloupes sus .i. drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	you must wrap it in a cloth, as long as it goes;
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as .ij. piés.	then the cap on the joint of the palm or wrist, and so you must do in the other hand, and in both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee,	And if the child's head is large and it is constricted at the exit, or it has a sharp pain accumulated,
si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	If it is necessary for you to stop the spasm, grip the spine between your fingers, press on the head and draw out the water.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	Or you can use the instrument called "almidach", from which the shape comes with the instruments or chapter that follows this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	And in the same way, if it has a large natural head;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles,	and then pull out the bones with tweezers,
et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and if the head of the shoulder pops out and is forced back in, it will be split open so that the moisture can escape.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot exit, then cut it out in pieces as best you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, then you must pierce it so that the moisture can flow out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the swelling is on his feet, and the pulse is light, and the pulse in the throat is weak.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a .i. drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is strained in the belly or the thigh, then you must strain it with one garment wrapped around your hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and press the belly or the thigh until the moisture that is in it runs out;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure,	and if the other members are dislocated and the head remains,
si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	let him put his hand into the wound up to the mouth of the wound;
puis i boute .i. oncine ou ij., et le trai fuer;	then I put in .I. hook or two, and pulled it out;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier,	and if the mouth of the wound is narrowed due to a hot abscess that has formed, one should not work on it,
ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	one must apply moist and greasy things;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and the doctor prescribes poultices, and bathes in warm water to soften and relax.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its side, and you can get it even, then administer what we have said about a live child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one has no power, then let the child be carried in pieces, and leave nothing of the afterbirth.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, if they are affected by what we have said about abscesses that come in childbirth;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if there is bleeding, let it be stopped with a bandage, and let the other treatments be applied.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman whose fetus had died within her belly; then another was sewn on top of it, and the other one died too.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, she developed an abscess in her armpit, which swelled up and opened, causing a foul discharge.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to treat her, and I thought about it for a long time, but couldn't find a way to heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I placed strong attracting plasters on her, and some bones came out, and after a few days, some more.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very amazed because there are no bones in one's belly.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought they were the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em miglior point;	I probed the wound and removed some bones, so that the woman was much improved.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and the woman lived a long time like this, and then she suddenly died.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have recorded this chapter only because when the masters encounter something strange, they know to seek help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring the dislocation back into place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	After that comes the form of the pulley, which is found in books; and with two turns at each of the two shoulders.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, the horns should be more subtle, made of ivory or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust .i. doi de large, et li marge des arbres .i. doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and its mouth should be two digits wide, and the edge of the trees one digit, and in length a palm and a half;
et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and in the two limbs there should be two adjustments of this same wood, which are firmly joined in one and the other, half a palm long or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.	and these two adjustments are built into the mouth of the saw to open when turning the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, which is more subtle and lighter, should be made of boxwood or ebony, according to the appearance of pliers;
et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;	and has two heads, two joints, as you see, the length of a palm, and two digits wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes,	and when you see to open the wound with all the instruments, then let the woman sit on a bed, her feet hanging and her legs spread wide;
puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	then put the two joints together in the wound, and hold the head of the instrument underneath between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand on the instrument as you did with the tweezers, according to the amount that you want to open the mouth of the wound, as long as the midwife does what she wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	These instruments are all surmounted, and their appearances are multiplied; and when the mirors have been prepared, the work is more swift, and men are higher for their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despair over the instrument until you have prepared it, for their necessity is inexcusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained at childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold her breath and then make her sneeze forcefully, and you must pinch her nose and mouth shut.Et quant ele vout esternuer, tu t’en vaas ad leus de la gosier et des entres; et si tu troves que ele retint la condisi ou l’alaine, tu la fai boire vin chaud, et si elle ne peuit boire, tu li mets del vin sur la narine.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she can't drink, put wine on her nose. And if she can't do that, it's still good.
Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take a pot and make an opening in the lid, and place herbs that can open the mouth of the wound, such as comfrey, rue, anise, chamomile, cassia, and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	all these herbs, or some of them, are cooked in water over the fire; then put one end of the pot into the wound, and the other end over the mouth of the wound,
et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	and let it steam so that the vapors enter the wound; then make her sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the pus does not come out easily.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature,	And if it persists after this treatment and does not subside, instruct the patient to soak their left hand in oil of sweet fennel or in a poultice of old age, and then let it air dry.
et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and seek out the second head; and when they have found it, grasp and gradually extend it straight so that the bone does not slip out.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	But it should be moved slightly to the right and left, and then pulled; it will come out easily.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the opening of the wound is narrow, we have described the treatment for sneezing and for fumigation with herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it is not of all that we have said, then beware that you do not make a mistake in treatment;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is appropriate that he who is at the mouth of the wound, you should tie him to the thigh of the woman, then you should cleanse with tetrafarmacon ointment;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	if she vomits and returns, but still, when she vomits, a bad odor comes to the stomach and head, and causes pain to the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	Then one should use suitable fumigations: some of the ancients have tried fumigation with watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument used to smoke out the woman for the retention of flowers and afterbirth, if it is like this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is made of glass, resembling a pipe, and one puts the small end into the vagina, and the wide end above the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and the smoke goes onto the charcoal, and it remains until it is used up, and one starts again with a new one.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the uterus
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born with an imperforate anus; instead, they have a narrow, slender opening.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	If necessary, the midwife should pierce that slender opening with her finger, and not cut it with a sharp instrument, and she should be careful not to tear it.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then she should put on wet linen, wine, and oil, and apply a poultice until it heals.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will close up again, put a piece of wood in the opening and leave it for a few days, then remove it when the child wants to go into the chamber.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	And sometimes this swelling comes suddenly from a wound or an abscess; then one must cover it suddenly: and it should be treated as we have said about the cane of splint.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula of the fundament
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that come from under the fundament are nodular and grow larger as they come from under the fundament, or in the space of two parts,
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	if there is one fistula or more; and when that nodule is old, it opens up and secretes a thick white pus or thin yellow fluid,
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and sometimes these are Persian ulcers; and they are caused by either flatulence or belching when the patient belches, and sometimes a fart jumps out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And if they have ulcers that pierce up to the bladder and halfway down the shaft of the penis; and they reach as far as the hip joint and the base of the scrotum.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And so one knows a Persian ulcer that pierces the anus and does not pierce through:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and you put your index finger into the anus, and insert a thin needle made of iron or steel into the ulcer when it is not twisted.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if there is crookedness, insert a tent of slender splint or a horsehair, until you feel the tent or hair at your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and there is no discharge or wind, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	you can be sure that it has not pierced through; then hasten to cure it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula has pierced as far as the bladder or the passage of urine, and urine escapes, and it cannot be stopped by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced up to the hip joint, then the tent is inserted up to that point.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is twisting and pain in the area around it, then it has moved from its place, and medicine or bandaging will not help;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and there is no cure for these piercings other than labor and the folly of those who interfere.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	In one that is neither pierced nor old, there is hope of recovery by means of iron, as I have experienced,
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and have the patient lie between your hands on his back; and lift his legs up to his thighs, and have his thighs inclined towards his belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then insert a tent of bronze or of wood if there is a bend, as far as you know the tent goes.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	If the patient feels it in his anus, then you must insert your index finger,
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and feel if the tent has pierced it; and if you feel between your finger and the anus, then you know it is perforated;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if you don't work on it then one cannot heal it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	We nevertheless can heal some, but that happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid one does, then one scorches the subtle cautery according to the width of the fistula, as has been said before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and he puts it all hot into the fistula, as far as it comes from the anus; and do this two or three times, as long as you know that the charred flesh is burned, which resembles a feather of a bird;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then cauterize with tents moistened in butter until that wound heals, then treat with ointment that hardens and seals.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If it is like this without pus, that is good. If not, it cannot be healed any other way.
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if the tent pierces and does not reach the bone that is in the foundation, and there is between your finger and the tent a thick covering of pus or of syrup, and you see the fistula below the covering of the heart;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	if the tip of the fistula is at the beginning, and fills up again before the tent, and then cauterize afterwards, until it reaches the top of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	and the tent will be delivered, and it will fall; then beware of those charred cars that look like a bird's feather, and nothing remains of them.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the vein bleeds, and the blood flows between you and the wound, then cauterize it with fire or with a medication.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	For the fire cautery gathers together two things: namely, the scorching of the charred flesh, and the stanching of blood and the drying up of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then the treatment of moist tents with butter or ground substances, until the flesh under the burns is healed and the burned cars fall off;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then heal the wound of the sudden, painful, hard, dry boils.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes from the depths of the fundament, and is separated from the body, put in two fingers or the fundaments, and investigate it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	If you feel the tent, and between two is the veil or the membrane, or it is close to piercing, there should be no sign of despair and hope, through the administration of one of three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	where you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it to the bone, or if you can, put in tent and treat it as before.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	do not go too deep, lest you cut the tissue holding the foundation, and let the exudate come out as it will.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it, as we have said.
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	by chance if it is healed, or you remove that covering and cleanse it after it has been cut down to the foundation, or by tent or by another pointed instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then cut out that piece of rotten wood which is in the wound, as much as you can.
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	then study how to restore the wound and stop the fistula from spreading through the body towards the anus: if it is a lighter thing for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And sometimes they are like this: and when you have put the tent in the fistula, and it is close to the anus on the skin side,
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	take a tent pierced at the tip according to this shape:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And insert a twisted thread into both, and insert the tent all along the thread in the fistula until it reaches the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is persistent at the edge of the anus, then pull out the thread from that opening as you would insert your finger into the anus.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	And pull on the head of the thread and bring the two shoulders together, squeezing them tightly, and leave it for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and restrain it sometimes, as long as the threads draw close to each other and stick;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then heal the wound until it is closed and clean.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not burst, then have it burst in every way you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For one must not bandage a wound that is so deep, but rather heal it, as we have said, until it is clean.Et s’ele est em parfont, si covient le lacement coper, et puis le cure, s’ele est em parfont, tant qu’il soit sanez.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spine of the thorn that they use to pierce the fistula is very sharp and pointed;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other hand not, because one does not grasp what one should not grasp, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Hemorrhoids are in two ways: either they are inside the anus, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and they ooze blood from time to time.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	And there is one or more of them, and they are outside the anus and at the top of the anus; but those that are outside have little moisture.
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	and then a little more yellow water or a little blood, and they have the color of the body;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the treatment of those who have them in the anus, it is that you instruct the patient to strain themselves to defecate into chambers, until the hemorrhoids come out, and they become visible;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	if it is large, you may cut it with tweezers or your fingernail, then pull it out by the root;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if they cannot be held with tweezers due to their moisture, then they can be held with a cloth or cotton, or a piece of chamois leather;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	take them out with your fingers, then crush and powder some hot powders that are in place of cauterization;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you can cauterize them as it is said in the chapter on cauterization, then treat with other treatments until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the bowels cannot move, then cleanse the patient with a harsh and sharp enema to clean what is in the bowels so that it can move freely;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	when the patients hold their breath, and if the thread is forced out from the bowel, then the treatment is minor;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and you should take them with your nail or tweezers and cut them, then treat them as we have said, until they are healed and fear the incision with iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	If you need to administer stitches in this way: take a twisted thread, and thread it onto a needle, then pull the thread above the needle, and pierce the needle from the other side, and turn both ends of the thread underneath the needle.
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and tighten the thread firmly, then tie a knot in the thread, and remove the needle, and do the same with all the others, and leave one to stop the flow of blood;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then place a damp cloth soaked in rose oil or cerate over the wound, and command the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then let it drop, and when they have fallen, then treat them with ointment and other remedies until they heal.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	drying from the heat or moisture of the bowels
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Drying of the bowels often occurs in the intestines due to natural constriction and when the disease is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	You should cut off the tip of a spatulum or your fingernail and apply it to the sore without letting it touch moisture.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then treat it until it is healed as it should be;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it cannot heal, then restart the cautery more fiercely than before, until it heals a lot, and let it be scalded;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it until it is healed.
dou fremit	where it trembles
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Ant is a small creature with a stinger under its body, and it goes deep underground.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	Sometimes the sting of the ant causes frostbite, and it feels like death, shivering throughout the body, more so in the hands than anywhere else.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a feather from an owl's wing, or a strong vulture's feather, and place this feather on the shivering, until the purple circle around the shivering disappears.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then return your hand to all of the feather, moving it around the shivering, and insert the feather deeply, and pull out the shivering from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see, make a needle of bronze or iron according to this form, and let it be slender beneath and broad above.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you wish, cauterize the wound, as it is before the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	Sometimes an enema is made of silver or brass, or molten copper or lead; and sometimes it is made with these small and large instruments, according to which they are made for someone.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those who are administered treatment for children and those who are feeble and in pain are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the small and large enema is above wide, where the bellies are tied according to this way:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	and it has an untying where the belly is tied, as you see, and the gut is pierced inside; and it has two openings on one side, and one on the other.;
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	and the belly where one puts the medicine is made of a beast's bladder or parchment, and it is pierced all around with small openings,
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and has between each aperture .I. finger's width of space, then weave into these apertures .I. strong thread of twisted thread in .X. or around, and tie the belly so that it is like a goat;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and when the medicine is inside, it lies against the instrument in front of a strong thread, then clysterize; and this is the shape of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot or too cold, and anoint the tip of the clyster with oil or egg yolk, or similar thing, then insert it gently;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	Then the minister squeezes it with both hands together until it is all voided, then pull out the clyster and let the patient lie on his side,
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if the medicine wants to go out, let it, as much as it can; and if he sleeps a night afterwards, it is even better help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you enema him for an illness of diarrhea, and the medicine wants to come out quickly, do it again until he is healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are in the anus, or an abscess, then the enema should be as gentle as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is how to make the gentle enema that will not hurt the skin:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have already discussed in the division the cure of wounds; now we will tell you about the cures with hands and medicine, according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse depending on how they are made, and depending on the location and the cause of the wound.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The objects that cause wounds are from stone, and cutting with a sword and knife, or a spear, staff, or arrow, or similar things.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	where they are made according to the locations on the body, such as wounds that occur on the neck, or head, or leg, or stomach, or liver, and similar organs;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and I will begin with simple head wounds, because the memory will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	I say that when a simple wound comes to the head, and the bone is not broken, take care if it is from a stone or similar object, and the skin is still broken and the wound is large,
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	and you should quickly doubt a hot abscess: if it makes the head bleeding immediately from the wound, and the bleeding is in the opposite direction of the damaged part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and prevent the patient from becoming bloated with wine and fatty foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not want to fast, then his food should be reduced, and he should not drink wine or eat meat;
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	and place a warm compress on the wound, if there are hot abscesses, soak cotton in rose oil only, or in astringent wine;
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	and if there is no hot abscess, place it on the wound, if it is fresh and bleeding, and has not been moved by the wind, powder, which I will describe in a little while;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if it has moved, put some ointments on it until it heals.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large, like that of a sword-cut and similar, and the lips cannot be approximated with tenting, then approximate them with suturing, as I will say for abdominal wounds, from the ribs up.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound is exposed to the bone, and gaping, and not holding together except by a thread, then cut it; then cure the wound with medicine, and restore hard flesh in place of skin,
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	and instruct the patient to eat coarse foods, such as eggs and cooked wheat, as well as meat, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find skin eruptions, and it is not on the bone, then scrape off all of it, and let it flow out, then heal it.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	and if there is an artery in the wound or vein, causing blood to flow without stopping, and it cannot be staunched by remedies, then tie off the artery, and if you find it dislocated, then bind it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	and if that does not help, then cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, the treatment is easy: you should apply this powder that heals as soon as the burn occurs.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the manner of the powder is thus: take frankincense one part; dragon's blood two parts; quicklime three parts, and mix the powder subtly.
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	And apply the wound, and press it firmly, until it is well healed and joined to all his blood;
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	and then dress it well, and leave it without dislodging, if it does not swell; for one does not remove the medicine until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And sometimes one makes this from quicklime only, when one does not have the incense or dragon's blood, but the fire should open the wound.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the wound has moved the powder, just as it is, put on some of this powder.
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but apply some digestive ointments or barley flour paste made with water and honey until it turns yellow.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it with other remedies until it heals.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if there is a fracture with the wound, and it is small, then extract it with small pincers;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you about fractures of the head afterward.
de la plaie dou col	of the wound on the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound is on the neck and it is simple, there is no difference between it and the one on the head, except that the nerves or arteries of the neck are cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the nerve, there should be no other treatment than leaving it alone and not putting anything that restricts it, because it hurts the nerves and makes them retreat.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	and do not put anything cold on the wound, for the substance of the nerves is cold, and their continuation is with the brain, which is the highest member;
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but let the medicine be warm, like hot water washed in cool water and mixed with rose oil, and cooked water also washed in cool water,
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other moist stones according to this manner, and moist ointments.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, then cut it and ligature it, and then treat it until it is healed.Et si li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and it is chapped and full of pus, then pierce it or a lower place.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	and if the artery is cut, and bleeding ensues, then ligature it, and let it be bound, and cauterized if necessary;
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	and if the spine of the throat is cut, or the windpipe, and the passage is blocked, by which food goes,
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	if it cuts through the cartilage above the Adam's apple, but does not touch the throat itself, then reset it according to its natural shape;
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then stretch it gently, and leave it for a few days, then treat it with healing ointments until it is healed;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if the wound has left an impression on the bone, then treat it thus;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	and if there are pieces of bone, then tie them tightly together as much as you can, and those that you cannot reach, leave them be until the wound has healed over them,
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	and let it heal and close up the opening;
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	and if the wound is fresh, then powder on the powder which I have described.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and there is a fistula, then treat it as I have said in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of a wound from a spear or knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it is a deep spear or knife wound, and the patient breathes with difficulty: then know that the wound is mortal;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and if it is not deep, and it is fresh with all its blood, then do not put the powder to it in the first hour, nor bind it for the blood that oozes out of it deeply.
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	and return to the body, and heal the wound;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but apply an attractive ointment, and bind it .ii. times a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you do not have ointment, put old cotton into the wound to absorb moisture,
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	and let the patient sleep on the wound for three days, or four, or more.
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if no spasm or tremor comes, nor bad twitching of the limbs,
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see these good signs, then know that the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then cure it with poultices and other remedies until it is completely healed;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	and if it cannot heal and function, then you know there is a fistula; treat it as one should.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife incision, and it is simple, or on the chest or back, then treat it as one who is in front;
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	if it is large, stitch it up; and if it is small, powder it, and if it has cut into the bone, and there are pieces sticking out, then clean the wound and pull out the foreign objects;
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not dislodged, then let the wound fester, so that the foreign objects will come out;
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	and for other wounds in other limbs, the judgement is as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	the rupture of the belly
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	There are great, medium, and small ruptures of the belly;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	of the great wound, sometimes the intestine, or the bowels, by which the entrails are exposed;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	and sewing is more difficult, and sometimes a small wound is worse than a large one,
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	because it is harder to sew up the intestines if they are not sewn up gradually, from warm to hot;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	and because the intestines swell as soon as they feel cold, they contract more with cautery,
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	and therefore it is better to cauterize the intestine at its own place than at other places. [II.13]
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	And know that dislocation of the belly occurs in four ways:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	the two common dislocations occur in the belly's suture;
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and the other dislocation of the body's wounds and two other unique dislocations are common to other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	And yet they are most commonly associated with the belly's suture, and I will describe each one and clarify:
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when a wound is small, and there is no intestine protruding,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	and it can be easily repaired, which is through one of the two methods:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	or because of the small size of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because the intestine is inflamed due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, heat it in this way:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	moisten a sponge or a soft cloth with lukewarm water,
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	or you can boil in water squills and cyprus and spice,
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and rose the intestines until their inflammation is relieved;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	and sometimes it makes this restraining wine, and it is changed to a soul for deflation.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the swelling depart, then moisten the intestines with water or old wine in which herbs have been cooked,
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	because through this, the entrance is blocked by a little thing;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	and if it cannot enter, they make a small hole in the instrument with which one cuts the hemorrhoids;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	and the first treatment is mud from the river,
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	that one should not cut without great necessity;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and this is the instrument for splitting it:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut inside the curve and not out, and see here the shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is enlarged, and the intestines jump out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	one puts it back in its natural shape and place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	if you have the power, for this is worth it.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is large and it is in the lower part of the abdomen,The following text is a medieval medical treatise written in Old French, around the 12th-13th centuries.
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	if you must make the patient lie on his back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and put his legs higher than his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	and if it is in the part below the belly,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	put the head and feet higher than the parts below,
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and so is the rupture of the belly in one of its two parts
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	put your understanding into this: that the ruptured part be higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	and thus one should manage both great and minor wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	For minor wounds, use what you are skilled in,
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	then have with you .i minister pity who dyes all the hair on his hand
et assemble les levres;	and pulls together the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and that is the common way of suturing,
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	and you should pierce an needle or more, according to the width of the wound,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then leaves a gap of about an inch at the head of the wound, and inserts a needle with a strong thread through it;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	and pierces the two heads of the skin with the two heads of the needle,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is under the skin inside, as far as you can make it pierce from that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and binds the two heads of the needle together with the fourth thread;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then draw it out with a double thread around the needle of 1/4 part
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	then join the 2 edges of the wound smoothly,
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and then leave 1 digit of space, and insert another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then tie the thread as you did with the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and do not cease doing this according to what you need of the needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until the entire wound is restrained;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	and let the needles be medium-sized, between thin and thick,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	because thin needles pierce all the flesh, and the too thick ones cannot enter well:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	they should therefore be moderate.
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and one must not push the needles too deep into the flesh and through the skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	so that they do not cut and open the wound before it heals.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	and then cover the heads of the needles with a layer so that they do not hurt the patient when he sleeps,
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and they use tents or cloth over the needles to hold them steady,
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and let it be until the wound is closed.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	and this way of sewing with needles is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because it requires only one needle or two.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second stitch is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	and is that you join the two heads of the skin and the two heads of the wound together with a needle and a strong, thin thread;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	And when you have pierced these heads all four together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	then put the needle back into the wound in the same way that one sews clothes;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and space between each stitch the thickness of a thumb nail;
ceste costure sevent li home,	this stitching is for men,
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	and I sewed up a wound that a man had on his belly,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	which was made by a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	was more than a palm wide,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and protruded intestines a good two palms long,
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	and the wound was in his belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I returned the intestine to where it had been 24 hours before,
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	and the wound was sewn up for fifteen days, and I treated it, and it healed.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And those who saw him believed that he would die, and this was a miracle:
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and I did not treat it with ointments, for I was in a place where none could be found, nor any medicine;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	and applied cotton wool to the wound twice a day, and washed it with honey water until it healed.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	Here I will tell you about two proper methods of sewing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	take the needle and thread it from outside to inside;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	once the needle has pierced the skin from right to right, then tie off the thread where you threaded the needle;
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	and have it pierce through from the inside out;
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	and the understanding of this sewing is that you sew as the furrier sews furs,
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	and that you leave once the edge on one side, and pull it back on the other, until the seam is complete.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of sewing, which Galen describes correctly,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	is such that they unite the two parts naturally,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	and apply one of the chief to the other chief, in such a way:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	stick a needle into the nearest vein, and make it pierce only that spot,
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	and leave the two chiefs of the syringe;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	then turn the needle and make it pierce from the outside part just to the inside,
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	that there are two kinds of dislocation;
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	then pierce both sides of the part affected up to the chest, in two other places that are on either side;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	and this is the best and most common method of suturing.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen says this, and some testify,
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	sew up the abdomen with .ij. needles, one in each;
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and you must thread one needle from one side and the other from the other, as those who sew up ulcers do;
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	and know that when there is a rupture in the belly,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	the stitches will be more painful than in other parts of the belly.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The diagnosis of the wound is the same as for other wounds.
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	It is that when you find the fresh wound full of blood, and the fire has moved it,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	then put back the intestine and the gut; then put on the cooling powder,
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	and if the fire has moved it, then put on some ointment that is present, until the wound heals;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and cut the thread, and sew up the wound, and the navel;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat the wound as with the others, until it is healed.
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	and if you have no medicine, apply old cotton, as soon as it begins to ooze pus,
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	and change it twice daily until it is healed.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you do not need any other medicine for various conditions when wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt that the wound will affect the principal members,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	then you should wet a light linen in warm tempered oil, or rose oil,
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and place it around the joints, and under the armpits;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	and if they feel pain or itching in the testicles, which often occurs,
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	if they are enemaed with warm wine, especially when the itching extends to the intestines;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	and it pierces inside; and you know that when it is the large intestine, it is easier to cure than the small intestine.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine which is called "young" cannot heal when it is raw,
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	and it is due to the abundance of veins that they are, and because of the subtlety of the whole body, and the closeness of its nature to nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the fat jumps out of the wound, then put it back inside just like the intestines, while it is fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	and if it is old and has become green or black, then you must tie off the area that is black so that bleeding does not occur;
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	because there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	then cut what is between the ligature,
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	and place the two ends of the thread hanging from the part below the wound to ease the extraction when the sutures are removed and the wound is closed.
de la routure dou boueil	of the thread
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are torn, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	if one can restore it in any way,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I saw a man was stabbed in the stomach with a spear;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	and the wound was on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and it became a fistula and discharged fluids, and he experienced both diarrhea and flatulence;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I applied treatment according to my abilities, and I did not cease sutilizing until he was healed and the wounds closed.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw that he was healing, I doubted that the patient had an evil in his belly:
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	and there was no evil in him, but he remained in better condition, eating and drinking;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	and some experimentarors said that when there is a small wound in the intestine, it must be bound in such a way:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	take thread from old testicles, then gather the lips of the wound,
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	and when the thread has opened the mouth, place it over the two lips,
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	so that it pulls the mouth closed again;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	and then tie the head, and it will hold so that it cannot come undone,
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	then apply another fomentation in the same manner as before, until the wound is completely healed.
et cout la plaie.	and then examine the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	If they pierce the intestines and do not harm the patient,
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	and one can tie the intestines with a thin thread that is cut from the intestine of an animal,
en teil maniere:	in such a way:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	take the end of this intestinal thread that is very charred,
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	and then tie to the end of this thread a thin, twisted flax thread,
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	then thread the needle and sew up the intestine, and then pull it back in;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	and this way of sewing up the fissure is not useless, according to the path of faith and hope.
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	and if the wound is great and wide, especially when it is in one of the internal veins, then there is no healing except through subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of a fistula, wherever it may be
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	Know that any wound or abscess, when it wakes up, is generally called a "fistula",
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	and likewise when it is swollen and returns bow-shaped.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	And a fistula is according to the verdant nodulation, a hard and white swelling, where one does not feel pain,
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	and is also swollen like the feather of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	and sometimes it is clear and bowed, and sometimes thick;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	sometimes little, and sometimes enough;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	and I have spoken of in the division of wounds, that any wound that is not cleaned and has no pus,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	this is only due to one of the eight causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	that is, by the smallness of blood or flesh;
ou por sa malice;	or for its malice;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or because there is hard charcoal within, and on the lips, that does not allow blisters to form;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	or because there is too much phlegm;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	or because the wound is putrid, and the matter is of poor quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	or medicine is not good in the treatment;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	or because the corruption is a kind of pestilence;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	or because the property in the region is tardy in digestion, and slow in health, and swollen by nature;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	or there are veins or bones:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	I have already shown all these causes, signs, and medical treatments for this disorder in the section on diseases of the head.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	Now I will tell you about the treatment for a fistula that is performed manually.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	You should know that a fistula can occur anywhere in the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	because there are fistulas that come from large veins, arteries, and nerves,
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or the sinus, or the intestine, or the bladder, or any of the sides,
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	or the spine in the back, or any joint of the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	and if it affects the principal member, and similar places.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all fistulas that are in this way are of grief sanation, and there is nothing but labor and ignorance;
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	and if there is any fistula that does not come up to where I have said, and you have faith in the cure,
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	and you see it, take a tent of bronze or iron, if the fistula is straight, so take it;
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	and if the fistula is crooked, then look for a thin, flexible tent made of lead,
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	because lead bends and moves around the curvature.
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	and if the fistula has many openings and you cannot explore it well with tenting,
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	if you cleanse it through one of the openings,
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	because moisture travels from one opening to another, and cleanses it;
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont,	then seek bleeding at your discretion, that you know if there is bone or nerve, and is cut through deeply,
et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	and ask the patient about the pain he feels when you press your hand down, and where he feels it most.
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine,	and once you know the exact location of the dislocation, whether it is near a joint, nerve, artery or vein,
ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit,	or in any of the places I've just described, then treat it according to what I've instructed.
et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	and remove any putrid flesh and rotten matter within.
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee,	and then the treatment until it is healed.
et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues,	And if the fistula is deep and in a good place, you must dig it out as deeply as you can,
puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule,	then put moist tents in the medicine until it reaches the head of the fistula,
tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	until the medicine corrodes the excess that remains at the bottom;
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then I apply warm compresses until it is healed;
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit,	and if it is not healed by that, then cauterize it as we have said,
et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	and if the bone is corrupted by the fistula, then cut it out.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If a vein or nerve troubles you in the principal limbs, as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee,	and if the bone is exposed, and there is decay and blackness, then treat it until the decay is completely removed,
puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	then clean it with warm water as long as it is necessary;
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant,	and if it is not healed and becomes swollen again as before,
saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	you should know that you have not gone to the spring:
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons,	If you uncover and desire as much as you are deep
et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	then remove all the corruption, then restore the place;
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	and if it is thus healed, that is good.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	If not, know that the corruption is too deep for you to reach;
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	if there is no other cause than weariness of nature
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles,	and if there is a small rotten bone, and you can pull it out with tweezers,
si l’estrai a .i. estrument covenauble a ceu,	if the extraction has an appropriate instrument for this purpose,
et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	and if there are many bones, pull them all out, not leaving one behind,
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour,	and if moisture causes it harm, and there is no error or fear,
si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	then cut and burn the moistness, and deliver the bones.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture,	And if you cannot remove them in an hour, then place something caustic over the wound,
et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os,	and let it sit until the pus has run around the bones,
et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	and then they will have easier access to the bones;
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse,	and if it is a large bone, such as those in the leg or thigh,
si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee,	then only remove the corruption until all of the darkness has been eliminated,
